01.22.2025 ADOPTED 
 
 
TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
 
TB Resolution 2025-129 
 
APPROVES SPECIAL EVENT CHAPTER 255 APPLICATION FOR NY MARINE 
RESCUE CENTER (RUN FOR THE RIDLEY 5K) 
 
Councilman Rothwell offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilman Kern 
 
WHEREAS, on January 7, 2025, Maxine Montello, on behalf of New York Marine 
Rescue Center, submitted a Chapter 255 Application for the purpose of conducting an 
Event Entitled “Run for the Ridley 5K”, Starting and ending off East Main Street, 
Riverhead, NY (See map attached), on October 18, 2025 between the hours of 5:00 am 
and 12:00 pm, rain or shine; and 
 
WHEREAS, the applicant has paid the requisite Chapter 255 Application fee of 
$175.00; and 
 
WHEREAS, a certificate of insurance naming the Town of Riverhead as an 
additional insured has been received; and   
 
NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED, that the Town Board of the Town of 
Riverhead hereby has classified the action as a Type II under SEQRA NYCRR 617.5 C 
(21) and requiring no further environmental review; and be it further 
 
RESOLVED, that the necessary tent permits must be obtained and any tent 
installations and all electric shall comply with the applicable provisions of the NFPA Life 
Safety Code (NFPA 101), the NFPA Temporary Membrane Structures/Tents (NFPA 
102) and the Fire Code of New York State; and be it further 
 
RESOLVED, that this approval is subject to the provisions of Riverhead Town 
Code Chapter 301-251 G (7) entitled “Signs” and any other section of the Riverhead 
Town Code that may pertain to this event; and be it further 
 
RESOLVED, that the Outdoor Safety Plan submitted with the applicant’s chapter 
255 application is subject to the review and approval of the Riverhead Fire Marshal; and 
be it further 
 
RESOLVED, that should it be determined that police and or fire marshal 
personnel and vehicle usage become necessary for this event, then in that instance, 
New York Marine Rescue Center agrees to pay the costs associated with same, which 
shall become due and payable upon delivery of an invoice to them for those additional 
costs; and be it further 
 
RESOLVED, that the Garbage/Trash/Rubbish Removal Plan submitted with the 
applicant’s Chapter 255 Application is subject to the review and approval of the 
Sanitation Department and be it further 
9.41
Packet Pg. 404
 
RESOLVED, that al l events taking place on Town property may be contingent 
upon the execution of a License Agreement with the Town of Riverhead within 7 days of 
the event and a fee of not less than $100.00; and be it further, 
 
RESOLVED, that all events taking place on Town property that will have the sale 
or consumption of alcohol are contingent on NYS Liquor Authority approval for on -site 
consumption; and be it further, 
 
RESOLVED, that the Town Supervisor is authorized to execute a license 
agreement for the use of Town prop erty as well as with participating alcohol service 
vendors in a form to be approved by the Town Attorney’s Office; and be it further,  
 
RESOLVED, that the Chapter 255 Application for the purpose of conducting the 
event Run for the Ridley 5K on October 18, 2025 is hereby approved; and be it further 
 
RESOLVED, that the Town Clerk is hereby authorized to forward a copy of this 
resolution Chief of Police, Edward Frost, Chief Fire Marshal, Andrew Smith and Maxine 
Montello mmontello@nymarinerescue.org, and be it further  
 
RESOLVED, that all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of 
this resolution from the electronic storage device and, if needed, a copy of same may be 
obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk.   
 
THE VOTE 
 
RESULT: ADOPTED [UNANIMOUS] 
MOVER: Kenneth Rothwell, Councilman 
SECONDER: Robert Kern, Councilman 
AYES: Hubbard, Rothwell, Kern, Merrifield, Waski

TB Resolution 2025-132 
 
RATIFIES AUTHORIZATION FOR THE TOWN ATTORNEY TO EXECUTE A 
RETAINER AGREEMENT WITH SOKOLOFF STERN LLP 
 
Councilwoman Waski offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilman Rothwell 
 
WHEREAS, the Office of the Town Attorney has recommended and requested 
that the Town Board authorize the Town Attorney to retain the services of Sokoloff Stern 
LLP to defend or otherwise appear on behalf of the Town of Riverhead and the 
members of t he Riverhead Town Board in an action commenced in United States 
District Court, Eastern District of New York, entitled Romano, et al. v. Town of 
Riverhead, et al., under Docket No: 24-cv-08910-ST.   
 
NOW, THEREFORE, BE IT RESOLVED , that the Town Board of t he Town of 
Riverhead hereby ratifies the appointment of Sokoloff Stern LLP to defend or appear in 
the above action commenced in United States District Court, Eastern District of New 
York, entitled Romano, et al. v. Town of Riverhead, et al., under Docket N o: 24 -cv-
08910-ST; and be it further, 
 
 RESOLVED, that the Town Board ratifies the authorization for the Town Attorney 
to execute the attached Retainer Agreement; and be it further, 
 
 RESOLVED, that the Town Clerk is hereby directed to forward a copy of th is 
resolution to the Accounting Department and the Office of the Town Attorney; and be it 
further,   
 
 RESOLVED, that all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of 
this resolution from the electronic storage device and, if needed, a certified copy of 
same may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk. 
 
THE VOTE 
 
RESULT: ADOPTED [UNANIMOUS] 
MOVER: Joann Waski, Councilwoman 
SECONDER: Kenneth Rothwell, Councilman 
AYES: Hubbard, Rothwell, Kern, Merrifield, Waski

01.22.2025 ADOPTED 
 
 
TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
 
TB Resolution 2025-133 
 
RATIFIES SETTLEMENT OF LEGAL ACTION AGAINST THE OWNERS OF 
PREMISES LOCATED AT 250 NEWTON AVE, RIVERHEAD, NEW YORK 
 
Councilman Rothwell offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilman Kern 
 
WHEREAS, a legal action was commenced in the name of the Town of Riverhead 
against the owners, tenants and occupants of the structure and property situated 250 
Newton Avenue, New York, in the Supreme Court of the State of New York under Index 
Number: 626569/2024, to enjoin the illegal use, occupancy and/or maintenance of said 
property and the structure situated upon said premises; and 
WHEREAS, the parties have reached a settlement of that legal action inclusive of all 
costs, expenses and interest; and 
WHEREAS, in light of the costs attendant to proceeding to a trial together with the 
uncertainties of litigation, the Town Attorney’s Office demanded, and received, certain terms 
of settlement, including penalties payable to the Town in the sum of $6,000.00. 
NOW, BE IT RESOLVED, that the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead be and 
hereby accepts and ratifies the settlement reached regarding legal action in the name of 
the Town of Riverhead against the owners, tenants and occupants of the structure and 
property situated at 250 Newton Avenue, Riverhead, New York, in the Supreme Court 
of the State of New York under Index Number: 626569/2024; and be it further,  
 
 RESOLVED, that the Office of the Town Attorney is hereby authorized to enter into a 
stipulation of settlement on behalf of the Town as well as any other documents necessary to 
effectuate the settlement of the litigation; and it is further; and be it further, 
 
 RESOLVED, that the Town Clerk is hereby directed to forward a certified copy of 
this resolution to the Accounting Department and the Office of the Town Attorney ; and be it 
further,  
 
RESOLVED, that all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of this 
resolution from the electronic storage device and, if needed, a certified copy of same 
may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk. 
 
THE VOTE
